SCENE_A0.SDT
SCENE_A1.SDT
World War III (2006)                   
In the year 2006 the virus DPX-a caused
a world wide epidemic. Over one billion
people, from all  regions of the world,
died within weeks of the first death.  
DPX-a  closely resembles  a virus  that
was artificially created  in 2002  as a
biological  weapon.  When  the outbreak
began, this man-made weapon was assumed
to be the cause.  The world's  military
powers  immediately  retaliated  with  
nuclear weapons.  Humanity entered its 
final nuclear war, World War III.      
About one month after the outbreak, the
truth about DPX-a was discovered by the
humans  hiding  deep  within  shelters 
built to withstand  nuclear fallout and
biological weapons. The virus was found
to have been released from its ancient 
resting  place  in  Antarctica  when a 
large  ice  shelf  melted  because  of 
global  warming.   How  the  virus     
propagated so quickly and took effect  
simultaneously  around  the  world  is 
still not known.                       
It was too late for those not protected
by the underground  shelters.  By this 
time,   the  virus  and  the  massive  
destruction  of  the  nuclear  war  had
nearly destroyed the humans on Earth's 
surface.
[Supplement: DPX-a outbreak details]   
Verification of time:                  
During  the  last  half  of  the  20th 
century, the world was faced with major
environmental  problems.   Industrial  
waste,  deforestation,  and other human
activities drove  many forms  of fauna 
and flora to extinction.  The sea level
was rising  steadily because of global 
warming.  In 2006  a large ice shelf in
Antarctica collapsed  and released the 
virus DPX-a,  which caused  a worldwide
disease  epidemic  and  the  subsequent
outbreak  of  World  War  III.  Nuclear
explosions  and  radiation  erased  the
world map and had a devastating impact 
on all life on Earth.                  
Cause of outbreak:                     
The  melting  of  an  ice  shelf  in   
Antarctica  released  an ancient virus,
DPX-a.                                 
Situation during the outbreak:         
A red smoke cloud was released when the
Antarctic ice-shelf disintegrated.     
This red smoke  quickly rose  into the 
upper  atmosphere,  carrying  the virus
DPX-a  with it.  The stratosphere  was 
contaminated  and  the Earth  turned a 
hazy red.  At the time, the true nature
of this cloud was misunderstood.       
Scientists thought  that  the red haze 
was associated with the destruction of 
the ozone layer.                       
?? Survivor project launched (2015)    
Only  a  few  people  reached  the     
underground  shelters.  Most  of  these
were  construction  workers  who  were 
constructing  the  sites.   Few  other 
humans survived  the epidemic  and the 
nuclear war.                           
The  Survivor  Project  was created  by
some of  the  best-equipped  workers to
find, rescue,  and assist all survivors
who  could  be found aboveground  or in
other underground shelters. A survey of
the  Earth's  environment  was  also   
undertaken.                            
Central government established (2030)  
The Survivor Project  found only  about
600,000 survivors worldwide,  including
those in underground shelters.  Most of
these survivors  had been infected with
viruses or exposed to radiation, and no
one had completely escaped  the ravages
of  the  disaster  of 2006.  Radiation 
still existed above ground at dangerous
levels.                                
The  idea  of a  central government was
first proposed in 2015.                
Because  the underground  shelters were
not  entirely  safe  and  clean,  the  
surviving  population  continued  to   
plummet.                               
By 2030,  when a central government was
finally established, only 35,847 people
remained alive on Earth.               
Survivor restoration team launched     
(2035)
After the establishment  of the central
government,  research  and  development
efforts  began   with  the  hope  of   
restoring  the  Earth's  environment.  
However, time was running out.  Because
of   radiation  leakage   and  other   
environmental   damage   caused   by   
centuries of pollution and the disaster
of 2006, researchers predicted that all
of the  underground  facilities  would 
become uninhabitable within 200 years. 
Two   major   scientific   teams   were
established  to  create  plans  for the
survival of the human race.            
Survivor restoration policy determined 
(2040)
Five  years  after  the launch  of the 
teams, two projects were proposed: the 
Seventh  Cross  Project  and  the Earth
Revive Project.   The 22,517  remaining
survivors  deliberated  the  merits of 
these  two  projects.  The Earth Revive
Project was selected  by more than 70% 
of the population.                     
The  Seventh  Cross  team, of which you
are a member,  could not  agree to the 
Earth  Revive  Project,  which required
hundreds  of  years  for  restoration. 
Because  we did not expect approval for
our project,  we have secretly secured 
our research laboratory in an abandoned
underground  shelter.  1,126  personnel
and  their families  have been moved to
this  laboratory  to begin  work on the
Seventh Cross project.                 
Earth Revive Project (2041)            
A survey in 2016,  ten years after the 
nuclear  disaster  of  2006, confirmed 
that  a few small  plants  and animals 
survived.  The survivors  were mutated 
by  exposure  to  radiation,  virus    
infection,  pollutants,  and  other    
environmental factors.
By  2020,   researchers  discovered    
additional  surviving  plants  and     
animals.  A more thorough survey found 
examples  from  each  of  the  major   
biological groups:                     
Invertebrates                          
Pisces                                 
Amphibians                             
Reptiles                               
Ornis                                  
Mammalia                               
The  environment  also showed  signs of
slow  but continual improvement. Levels
of contaminants were dropping.         
This study  made clear that restoration
of  the  earth's  ecosystem  could     
eventually  lead  to recovery  from the
environmental contamination. An attempt
to  artificially  recreate  the earth's
ecosystem  could have a negative effect
on this natural restoration process.   
The survivors decided  to let the Earth
restore  itself   with  minimal  human 
involvement.  The  Earth Revive Project
proposed  moving the population  into a
large  spacecraft  in orbit  around the
Earth.  The remainder of the human race
would  wait out the estimated 500 years
required  for  the Earth's  recovery in
cryogenic (cold) sleep.                
To promote normalization of the earth's
ecosystem,   an  intelligent  robotic  
monitoring  vessel  was proposed.  This
vessel  would  track  dangerous  genes,
including   those   mutated   through  
radiation  or virus infection,  and use
Neo Bionoid technology to eradicate any
such genes.                            
This  project  was  completed  in  2070
after 29 years of work constructing the
large spacecraft,  monitoring vessel,  
and Neo Bionoid.                       
Seventh Cross Project (2100)           
The Seventh Cross Project  continued in
secret  and  was launched  in 2100. The
Seventh Cross project  is  still in    
progress.
[Project overview]                     
The  Seventh Cross Project  team  feels
that the risk of  waiting for the Earth
to restore itself  while humanity waits
in  cryogenic  sleep  is  too high.  We
propose to modify existing human DNA to
survive in Earth's current contaminated
environment.                           
[Project procedure]                    
Create   multiple    experimental      
protohumans,  based on human DNA, which
can  rapidly  evolve  and  mutate  in  
adaptation to the environment.  Release
these experimental protohumans onto the
Earth's surface.                       
The protohumans  will be transferred in
sequence  through six biological areas.
Each  area  is  designed  to  encourage
reproduction  and rapid evolution while
protecting the protohumans from certain
harmful organisms.  When they reach the
sixth area,  the protohumans  will have
advanced  to become  primates  that are
similar  to  humans.  The  state  of   
evolution of the protohumans is checked
during each transfer,  and their DNA is
corrected accordingly.                 
When  the  DNA  structure  of  the     
protohumans  reaches  the  level  of   
advanced  primates  compatible  with   
humans,  the  DNA  for adapting  to the
environment  will be extracted and then
embedded  in the DNA of human sperm and
egg cells.  As a result,  we hope  that
humans  will  evolve  into  a new breed
that  can  adapt  to any change  in the
environment.                           
The chance  that a new advanced primate
will  survive  in this project  is only
1 in 810,000. To increase the odds, the
protohumans  are provided  with special
abilities through genetic manipulation.
Ironically,  this  genetic  technology 
emerged from the study of DNA extracted
from deformed organisms contaminated by
radiation.
